<!-- likebox replacement -->\n            <div id=\"maincontent\" class=\"homepage\">\n                <div id=\"hp_m_cont\">\n                    <div id=\"hp_r_col\">\n                        <div id=\"notice\">\n                            <h2>Solicitation Deadlines Extended\n                            \n                            </h2>\n                            <p>NIJ has extended the deadlines for two solicitations:\n                            \n                            </p>\n                            <ul>\n                                <li>\n                                    <a href=\"/funding/Documents/solicitations/NIJ-2017-12043.pdf\">\n                                        <em>Research and Evaluation on Drugs and Crime \n                                        \n                                        </em>\n                                    </a>\n\nnow will close on April 24, 2017.                                                                </li>\n                                <li>\n                                    <a href=\"/funding/Documents/solicitations/NIJ-2017-11481.pdf\">\n                                        <em>Research and Evaluation in Safety, Health,  and Wellness in the Criminal Justice System\n                                        \n                                        </em>\n                                    </a>\n\n now will close on May 8, 2017.                                                                </li>\n                            </ul>\n                        </div>\n                        <div id=\"highlights\">\n                            <h2 class=\"highlights_2\">Highlights\n                            \n                            \n                            \n                            \n                            \n                            \n                            \n                            \n                            \n                            \n                            \n                            \n                            \n                            \n                            \n                            \n                            \n                            \n                            \n                            \n                            \n                            \n                            </h2>\n                            <!-- ALL HIGHLIGHTS BEGIN -->\n                            <div class=\"accordbox openlanguage\" id=\"added04-19-2017\" headerindex=\"0h\"><span class=\"accordprefix\"></span>\n<span class=\"accordbox_header\">\n<a href=\"#\" class=\"accordboxlink\">Funding: Sexual Assault Forensic Evidence-Inventory, Tracking, and Reporting</a></span><span class=\"accordsuffix\"></span></div>\n        <div class=\"accordboxcontent\" contentindex=\"0c\" style=\"display: block;\">\n          <div class=\"ac_content\">\n            <p class=\"first\">Many law enforcement agencies do not have computerized systems to track the processing of a Sexual Assault Kit (SAK). This funding will assist eligible states, units of local government, and tribal governments to inventory, track, and report all untested and unsubmitted SAKs and help these jurisdictions ensure accountability and transparency for the collection, processing and testing of SAKs.</p>\n<p><a href=\"/funding/Documents/solicitations/NIJ-2017-11605.pdf\">Review the solicitation</a>. Applications are due April 28, 2017.</p>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n        <div style=\"height: 2px; background-color: #ffffff;\"></div>\n                            <div class=\"accordbox closedlanguage\" id=\"added04-04-2017\" headerindex=\"1h\"><span class=\"accordprefix\"><img src=\"/Style Library/Images/home-styles/1_right_arrow.gif\" alt=\"bullet\"> </span>\n                                <span class=\"accordbox_header\">\n                                    <a href=\"#\" class=\"accordboxlink\">Supporting Forensic Science Is a Priority at the National Institute of Justice\n\n                                    </a>\n                                </span>\n                            <span class=\"accordsuffix\"></span></div>\n                            <div class=\"accordboxcontent\" contentindex=\"1c\" style=\"display: none;\">\n                                <div class=\"ac_content\">\n                                    <p class=\"first\">NIJ is the largest support agency in the United States for forensic laboratory technical assistance, and offers the only extramural grant program in the nation dedicated to forensic science research, development, and evaluation.\n                                    </p>\n                                    <p>\n\n In a new Directors Corner, Acting Director Howard Spivak summarizes NIJs major contributions in strengthening the forensic science enterprise and restoring trust in the scientific underpinnings of the varied forensic science disciplines.\n\n                                    </p>\n                                    <p>\n                                        <a          <a class=\"mainNavLink tb_h a_tp selected\" href=\"#\" id=\"featured_topic\" name=\"featured_topic\">Featured Topic \n                                    \n                                    \n                                    \n                                    \n                                    \n                                    \n                                    \n                                    \n                                    \n                                    \n                                    \n                                    \n                                    </a>\n                                    <div style=\"display: block;\" class=\"content\" id=\"featured_topic_content\">\n                                        <!-- PASTE FEATURE BEGIN -->\n                                        \t\t\t\t<h2 class=\"p_h2\" id=\"posted04-19-2017\">Sexual Assault Kits: Using Science to Find Solutions</h2>\n\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"first\">NIJ supports a range of studies related to sexual assault, especially research related to the processing and testing of sexual assault kits. NIJ has worked with a number of cities  Los Angeles, New Orleans, Detroit, Houston, and others  in leading the way toward change.\n</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"/unsubmitted-kits/Pages/default.aspx\">Check out an interactive web poster</a> to learn all about how science is improving the effectiveness of our nations response to sexual assault. </p>\n\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"/unsubmitted-kits/Pages/default.aspx\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<img src=\"http://nij.gov/PublishingImages/features/unsubmitted-kits.jpg\" alt=\"Sexual Assault Kits: Using Science to Find Solutions\"></a>\n                                        <!-- PASTE FEATURE END -->\n                                    </div>\n                                    <!-- Closes Feature -->\n id=\"promotions\">\n                        <div id=\"promotions_interior\">\n                            <div id=\"promotionsright\" class=\"c7\">\n                               <h3>Reconstructing Mass Disasters</h3>\n\t\t\t                <img src=\"/publishingimages/promotions/skeletal-reconstruction.jpg\" alt=\"Our goal is to make [skeletal reconstruction] easier for law enforcement and paleoanthropology. Mahamed Mahfouz, Principal Investigator\">\n              <p class=\"img-att\">NIJ image (see <a href=\"http://nij.gov/publications/pages/reuse-policy.aspx\">reuse policy)</a>. </p>\n              <p>A new software, created with the support of NIJ, will aid in the reconstruction of fragmented bones, with a focus on mixed fragments from multiple individuals. This work may eventually automate the process of reconstructing remains.</p>\n              <p><a href=\"/topics/forensics/evidence/pathology/Pages/reconstructing-fragmentary-skeletal-remains.aspx?utm_source=promo&amp;utm_medium=homepage&amp;utm_campaign=article\">Read more</a>.</p>\n                            </div>\n                            <!-- /promotionsright -->\n                            <div id=\"promotionsleft\" class=\"c9\" style=\"height: 400px;\">\n<h3>Progress on Testing Kits</h3>\n\t\t\t   <iframe src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/nR6uxdaFVDA?rel=0?ecver=2\" width=\"325\" height=\"200\" frameborder=\"0\" _fsrb=\"true\"></iframe>\t\t\t  \n Privacy Policy</a>&nbsp;<a class=\"exitLink\" href=\"https://justice.gov/legalpolicies.htm#other\">Exit Notice</a></p>\n\n              <p>Learn about the importance of utilizing available resources, including research and support from NIJ, in making progress towards processing untested sexual assault kits.</p>\n              <p><a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=nR6uxdaFVDA\"
